(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,i,j,k,l) -> (c,i,e,a,j,h,b,k,g,d,f:N)(l:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,i,j,k) -> (i,e,a,j,h,b,k,g,d,f:N)(c:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,i,j) -> (d,a,i,g,b,j,h,c,e:N)(f:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h,i) -> (a,h,f,b,i,g,c,e:N)(d:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f,g,h) -> (h,f,b,a,e,c,d:N)(g:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f,g) -> (e,b,a,f,c,d:N)(g:T)
(a,b,c,d,e,f) -> (b,a,f,c,d:N)(e:T)
(a,b,c,d,e) -> (a,c,e,d:N)(b:T)
(a,b,c,d) -> (b,d,c:N)(a:T)
(a,b,c) -> (c,b:N)(a:T)
(a,b) -> (a:N)(b:T)
(a) -> (a:T)
(a) -> (0,a:T)
(a) -> (0,a:T)
